      return self.index < self.args.len;\n   894→    }\n   895→\n   896→    fn peek(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n   897→        if (self.index >= self.args.len) return null;\n   898→        return self.args[self.index];\n   899→    }\n   900→\n   901→    fn next(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n   902→        if (self.index >= self.args.len) return null;\n   903→        const arg = self.args[self.index];\n   904→        self.index += 1;\n   905→        return arg;\n   906→    }\n   907→\n   908→    /// Skip a peeked argument (used after checking with peek() and wanting to consume it).\n   909→    fn skip(self: *Self) void {\n   910→        if (self.index < self.args.len) {\n   911→            self.index += 1;\n   912→        }\n   913→    }\n   914→\n   915→    /// Check if current arg matches a flag, and if so consume it and return true.\n   916→    fn consumeFlag(self: *Self, short: ?[]const u8, long: []const u8) bool {\n   917→        const arg = self.peek() orelse return false;\n   918→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, long) or (short != null and std.mem.eql(u8, arg, short.?))) {\n   919→            self.skip();\n   920→            return true;\n   921→        }\n   922→        return false;\n   923→    }\n   924→\n   925→    /// Parse a u32 value after consuming a flag. Returns null if missing, error if invalid.\n   926→    fn consumeU32(self: *Self) ParseError!?u32 {\n   927→        const val = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n   928→        return std.fmt.parseInt(u32, val, 10) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n   929→    }\n   930→\n   931→    /// Parse an optional --limit/-n flag, returning the value if present.\n   932→    fn parseLimitFlag(self: *Self) ParseError!?u32 {\n   933→        if (self.consumeFlag(\"-n\", \"--limit\")) {\n   934→            return try self.consumeU32();\n   935→        }\n   936→        return null;\n   937→    }\n   938→\n   939→    /// Returns the next arg if it's a positional (doesn't start with \"-\"), otherwise null.\n   940→    fn peekPositional(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n   941→        const arg = self.peek() orelse return null;\n   942→        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, arg, \"-\")) return null;\n   943→        return arg;\n   944→    }\n   945→};\n   946→\n   947→// Tests\n 281→    pub fn list(self: *Self, filters: ListFilters) ![]Issue {\n   282→        var results: std.ArrayListUnmanaged(Issue) = .{};\n   283→        errdefer {\n   284→            for (results.items)           }\n   300→            if (filters.priority) |p| {\n   301→                if (issue.priority.value != p.value) continue;\n   302→            }\n   303→            if (filters.issue_type) |t| order_desc: bool,\n   328→        };\n   329→        const ctx = SortContext{ .order_by = filters.order_by, .order_desc = filters.order_desc };\n   330→\n   331→        std.mem.sortUnstable(Issue, results.items, ctx, struct {\n   332→            fn lessThan(c: SortContext, a: Issue, b: Issue) bool {\n   333→                const cmp: i64 = switch (c.order_by) {\n   334→                    .created_at => a.created_at.value - b.created_at.value,\n   335→                    .updated_at => a.updated_at.value - b.updated_at.value,\n   336→                    .priority => @as(i64, a.priority.value) - @as(i64, b.priority.value),\n   337→                };\n   338→                return if (c.order_desc) cmp > 0 else cmp < 0;\n   339→            }\n   340→        }.lessThan);\n   341→\n   342→        // Apply offset and limit\n   343→        var start: usize = 0;\n   344→        if (filters.offset) |off| {\n   345→            start = @min(off, results.items.len);\n   346→        }\n   347→\n   348→        var end: usize = results.items.len;\n   349→        if (filters.limit) |lim| {\n   350→            end = @min(start + lim, results.items.len);\n   351→        }\n   352→\n self.allocator.dupe(Issue, results.items[start..end]);\n   363→        results.deinit(self.allocator);\n   364→        return slice;\n   365→    }\n   366→\n   367→    /// Result from counting   374→    pub fn count(self: *Self, group_by: ?GroupBy) ![]CountResult {\n   375→        var counts: std.StringHashMapUnmanaged(u64) = .{};\n   376→        defer counts.deinit(self.allocator);\n   377→\n   378→        for (self.issues.items) |issue| {\n   379→            if (statusEql(issue.status, .tombstone)) continue;\n   380→\n   381→            const key_str: []const u8 = if (group_by) |g| results.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator);\n   414→    }\n   415→\n   416→    pub const GroupBy = enum {\n   417→        status,\n   418→        priority,\n   419→        issue_type,\n   420→ 444→\n   445→    /// Add a label to an issue.\n   446→    pub fn addLabel(self: *Self, issue_id: []const u8, label: []const u8) !void {\n   447→        const idx = self.id_index.get(issue_id) orelse Self {\n   100→        return .{\n   101→            .mode = mode,\n   102→            .toon = false,\n   103→            .stdout = std.fs.File.stdout(),\n   104→            .stderr = std.fs.File.stderr(),\n   105→            .allocator = allocator,\n   106→        };\n   107→    }\n   108→\n   109→    /// Initialize for testing with custom file handles.\n   110→    pub fn initForTesting(allocator: std.mem.Allocator, mode: OutputMode, stdout: std.fs.File, stderr: std.fs.File) Self {\n   111→        return .{\n   112→            .mode = mode,\n   113→            .toon = false,\n   114→            .stdout = stdout,\n   115→            .stderr = stderr,\n   116→            .allocator = allocator,\n   117→        };\n   118→    }\n   119→\n   120→    // ========================================================================\n   121→    // Issue Display\n   122→    // ========================================================================\n   123→\n   124→    /// Print a single issue in the appropriate format.\n   125→    pub fn printIssue(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n   126→        switch (self.mode) {\n   127→            .json => try self.printIssueJson(issue),\n   128→            .quiet => try self.printIssueQuiet(issue),\n   129→            .rich => try self.printIssueRich(issue),\n   130→            .plain => try self.printIssuePlain(issue),\n   131→        }\n   132→    }\n   133→\n   134→    /// Print a list of issues in the appropriate format.\n   135→    pub fn printIssueList(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n   136→        switch (self.mode) {\n   137→            .json => try self.printIssueListJson(issues),\n   138→            .quiet => try self.printIssueListQuiet(issues),\n   139→            .rich => try self.printIssueListRich(issues),\n   140→            .plain => try self.printIssueListPlain(issues),\n   141→        }\n   142→    }\n   143→\n   144→    // ========================================================================\n   145→    // Generic Messages\n   146→    // ========================================================================\n   147→\n   148→    /// Print a formatted message to stdout.\n   149→    pub fn print(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n   150→        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n   151→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt, args);\n   152→        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n   153→        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n   154→    }\n   155→\n   156→    /// Print a formatted message to stdout with newline.\n   157→    pub fn println(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n   158→        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n   159→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt ++ \"\\n\", args);\n   160→        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n   161→        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n   162→    }\n   163→\n   164→    /// Print a success message (green in rich mode).\n   165→    pub fn success(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n   166→        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n   167→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stdout.writeAll(Color.green);\n   168→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt, args);\n   169→        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n   170→        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n   171→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stdout.writeAll(Color.reset);\n   172→        try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   173→    }\n   174→\n   175→    /// Print an error message to stderr (red in rich mode).\n   176→    pub fn err(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n   177→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stderr.writeAll(Color.red);\n   178→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, \"error: \" ++ fmt, args);\n   179→        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n   180→        try self.stderr.writeAll(msg);\n   181→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stderr.writeAll(Color.reset);\n   182→        try self.stderr.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   183→    }\n   184→\n   185→    /// Print a warning message to stderr (yellow in rich mode).\n   186→    pub fn warn(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n   187→        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n   188→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stderr.writeAll(Color.yellow);\n   189→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, \"warning: \" ++ fmt, args);\n   190→        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n   191→        try self.stderr.writeAll(msg);\n   192→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stderr.writeAll(Color.reset);\n   193→        try self.stderr.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   194→    }\n   195→\n   196→    /// Print an info message (cyan in rich mode).\n   197→    pub fn info(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n   198→        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n   199→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stdout.writeAll(Color.cyan);\n   200→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt, args);\n   201→        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n   202→        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n   203→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stdout.writeAll(Color.reset);\n   204→        try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   205→    }\n   206→\n   207→    /// Print raw bytes to stdout (bypasses mode checks).\n   208→    pub fn raw(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) !void {\n   209→        try self.stdout.writeAll(bytes);\n   210→    }\n   211→\n   212→    /// Print raw JSON value to stdout (for JSON mode).\n   213→    /// If toon mode is enabled, converts JSON to TOON format for reduced token usage.\n   214→    pub fn printJson(self: *Self, value: anytype) !void {\n   215→        const json_bytes = try std.json.Stringify.valueAlloc(self.allocator, value, .{});\n   216→        defer self.allocator.free(json_bytes);\n   217→\n   218→        if (self.toon) {\n   219→            const toon = @import(\"toon_zig\");\n   220→            const toon_bytes = toon.jsonToToon(self.allocator, json_bytes) catch |convert_err| {\n   221→                try self.stderr.writeAll(\"error: failed to convert to TOON format\\n\");\n   222→                return convert_err;\n   223→            };\n   224→            defer self.allocator.free(toon_bytes);\n   225→            try self.stdout.writeAll(toon_bytes);\n   226→        } else {\n   227→            try self.stdout.writeAll(json_bytes);\n   228→        }\n   229→        try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   230→    }\n   231→\n   232→    // ========================================================================\n   233→    // JSON Mode Helpers\n   234→    // ========================================================================\n   235→\n   236→    fn printIssueJson(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n   237→        try self.printJson(issue);\n   238→    }\n   239→\n   240→    fn printIssueListJson(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n   241→        try self.printJson(issues);\n   242→    }\n   243→\n   244→    // ========================================================================\n   245→    // Plain Mode Helpers\n   246→    // ========================================================================\n   247→\n   248→    fn printIssuePlain(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n   249→        try self.writeFormatted(\"ID: {s}\\n\", .{issue.id});\n   250→        try self.writeFormatted(\"Title: {s}\\n\", .{issue.title});\n   251→        try self.writeFormatted(\"Status: {s}\\n\", .{issue.status.toString()});\n   252→        try self.writeFormatted(\"Priority: {s}\\n\", .{issue.priority.toString()});\n   253→        try self.writeFormatted(\"Type: {s}\\n\", .{issue.issue_type.toString()});\n   254→\n   255→        if (issue.description) |desc| {\n   256→            try self.writeFormatted(\"Description: {s}\\n\", .{desc});\n   257→        }\n   258→        if (issue.assignee) |assignee| {\n   259→            try self.writeFormatted(\"Assignee: {s}\\n\", .{assignee});\n   260→        }\n   261→        if (issue.labels.len > 0) {\n   262→            try self.stdout.writeAll(\"Labels: \");\n   263→            for (issue.labels, 0..) |label, i| {\n   264→                if (i > 0) try self.stdout.writeAll(\", \");\n   265→                try self.stdout.writeAll(label);\n   266→            }\n   267→            try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   268→        }\n   269→        if (issue.due_at.value) |due| {\n   270→            try self.writeFormatted(\"Due: {d}\\n\", .{due});\n   271→        }\n   272→\n   273→        try self.writeFormatted(\"Created: {d}\\n\", .{issue.created_at.value});\n   274→        try self.writeFormatted(\"Updated: {d}\\n\", .{issue.updated_at.value});\n   275→    }\n   276→\n   277→    fn printIssueListPlain(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n   278→        for (issues) |issue| {\n   279→            const status_abbrev = abbreviateStatus(issue.status);\n   280→            try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}  [{s}] {s}\\n\", .{\n   281→                issue.id,\n   282→                status_abbrev,\n   283→                issue.title,\n   284→            });\n   285→        }\n   286→    }\n   287→\n   288→    // ========================================================================\n   289→    // Rich Mode Helpers (ANSI colors)\n   290→    // ========================================================================\n   291→\n   292→    fn printIssueRich(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n   293→        // Bold ID\n   294→        try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ Color.bold, issue.id, Color.reset });\n   295→\n   296→        // Title\n   297→        try self.writeFormatted(\"  {s}\\n\", .{issue.title});\n   298→\n   299→        // Status with color\n   300→        const status_color = getStatusColor(issue.status);\n   301→        try self.writeFormatted(\"  Status: {s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ status_color, issue.status.toString(), Color.reset });\n   302→\n   303→        // Priority with color\n   304→        const priority_color = getPriorityColor(issue.priority);\n   305→        try self.writeFormatted(\"  Priority: {s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ priority_color, issue.priority.toString(), Color.reset });\n   306→\n   307→        // Type\n   308→        try self.writeFormatted(\"  Type: {s}\\n\", .{issue.issue_type.toString()});\n   309→\n   310→        // Optional fields\n   311→        if (issue.description) |desc| {\n   312→            try self.writeFormatted(\"  Description: {s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ Color.dim, desc, Color.reset });\n   313→        }\n   314→        if (issue.assignee) |assignee| {\n   315→            try self.writeFormatted(\"  Assignee: {s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ Color.cyan, assignee, Color.reset });\n   316→        }\n   317→        if (issue.labels.len > 0) {\n   318→            try self.stdout.writeAll(\"  Labels: \");\n   319→            for (issue.labels, 0..) |label, i| {\n   320→                if (i > 0) try self.stdout.writeAll(\", \");\n   321→                try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}{s}{s}\", .{ Color.magenta, label, Color.reset });\n   322→            }\n   323→            try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   324→        }\n   325→    }\n   326→\n   327→    fn printIssueListRich(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n   328→        for (issues) |issue| {\n   329→            const status_color = getStatusColor(issue.status);\n   330→            const priority_color = getPriorityColor(issue.priority);\n   331→            const status_abbrev = abbreviateStatus(issue.status);\n   332→\n   333→            try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}{s}{s}  {s}[{s}]{s}  {s}{s}{s}  {s}\\n\", .{\n   334→                Color.bold,\n   335→                issue.id,\n   336→                Color.reset,\n   337→                status_color,\n   338→                status_abbrev,\n   339→                Color.reset,\n   340→                priority_color,\n   341→                priorityIndicator(issue.priority),\n   342→                Color.reset,\n   343→                issue.title,\n   344→            });\n   345→        }\n   346→    }\n   347→\n   348→    // ========================================================================\n   349→    // Quiet Mode Helpers\n   350→    // ========================================================================\n   351→\n   352→    fn printIssueQuiet(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n   353→        try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}\\n\", .{issue.id});\n   354→    }\n   355→\n   356→    fn printIssueListQuiet(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n   357→        for (issues) |issue| {\n   358→            try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}\\n\", .{issue.id});\n   359→        }\n   360→    }\n   361→\n   362→    // ========================================================================\n   363→    // Internal Helpers\n   364→    // ========================================================================\n   365→\n   366→    fn writeFormatted(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n   367→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt, args);\n   368→        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n   369→        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n   370→    }\n   371→};\n   372→\n   373→// ============================================================================\n   374→// Helper Functions\n   375→// ============================================================================\n   376→\n   377→/// Check if NO_COLOR environment variable is set (cross-platform).\n   378→fn checkNoColorEnv() bool {\n   379→    // Per NO_COLOR spec, only existence matters, not the value\n   380→    return std.process.hasEnvVarConstant(\"NO_COLOR\");\n   381→}\n   382→\n   383→/// Get ANSI color for a status.\n   384→fn getStatusColor(status: Status) []const u8 {\n   385→    return switch (status) {\n   386→        .open => Color.green,\n   387→        .in_progress => Color.yellow,\n   388→        .blocked => Color.red,\n   389→        .deferred => Color.gray,\n   390→        .closed => Color.gray,\n   391→        .tombstone => Color.dim,\n   392→        .pinned => Color.bright_cyan,\n   393→        .custom => Color.blue,\n   394→    };\n   395→}\n   396→\n   397→/// Get ANSI color for a priority.\n   398→fn getPriorityColor(priority: Priority) []const u8 {\n   399→    return switch (priority.value) {\n   400→        0 => Color.bright_red, // critical\n   401→        1 => Color.red, // high\n   402→        2 => Color.yellow, // medium\n   403→        3 => Color.green, // low\n   404→        4 => Color.gray, // backlog\n   405→        else => Color.reset,\n   406→    };\n   407→}\n   408→\n   409→/// Get short status abbreviation.\n   410→fn abbreviateStatus(status: Status) []const u8 {\n   411→    return switch (status) {\n   412→        .open => \"OPEN\",\n   413→        .in_progress => \"PROG\",\n   414→        .blocked => \"BLKD\",\n   415→        .deferred => \"DEFR\",\n   416→        .closed => \"DONE\",\n   417→        .tombstone => \"DEL \",\n   418→        .pinned => \"PIN \",\n   419→        .custom => \"CUST\",\n   420→    };\n   421→}\n   422→\n   423→/// Get priority indicator symbol.\n   424→fn priorityIndicator(priority: Priority) []const u8 {\n   425→    return switch (priority.value) {\n   426→        0 => \"!!!\",\n   427→        1 => \"!! \",\n   428→        2 => \"!  \",\n   429→        3 => \".  \",\n   430→        4 => \"   \",\n   431→        else => \"   \",\n   432→    };\n   433→}\n   434→\n   435→// ============================================================================\n   436→// Tests\n   437→// ============================================================================\n   438→\n   439→test \"OutputMode enum values\" {\n   440→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.plain, OutputMode.plain);\n   441→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.rich, OutputMode.rich);\n   442→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.json, OutputMode.json);\n   443→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.quiet, OutputMode.quiet);\n   444→}\n   445→\n   446→test \"Output.init with json option\" {\n   447→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   448→    const opts = OutputOptions{ .json = true };\n   449→    const output = Output.init(allocator, opts);\n   450→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.json, output.mode);\n   451→    try std.testing.expect(!output.toon);\n   452→}\n   453→\n   454→test \"Output.init with toon option\" {\n   455→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   456→    const opts = OutputOptions{ .toon = true };\n   457→    const output = Output.init(allocator, opts);\n   458→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.json, output.mode);\n   459→    try std.testing.expect(output.toon);\n   460→}\n   461→\n   462→test \"Output.init with quiet option\" {\n   463→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   464→    const opts = OutputOptions{ .quiet = true };\n   465→    const output = Output.init(allocator, opts);\n   466→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.quiet, output.mode);\n   467→}\n   468→\n   469→test \"Output.init with no_color option forces plain mode\" {\n   470→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   471→    const opts = OutputOptions{ .no_color = true };\n   472→    const output = Output.init(allocator, opts);\n   473→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.plain, output.mode);\n   474→}\n   475→\n   476→test \"Output.init json overrides quiet\" {\n   477→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   478→    const opts = OutputOptions{ .json = true, .quiet = true };\n   479→    const output = Output.init(allocator, opts);\n   480→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.json, output.mode);\n   481→}\n   482→\n   483→test \"Output.initWithMode sets explicit mode\" {\n   484→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   485→    const output = Output.initWithMode(allocator, .rich);\n   486→    try std.testing.expectEqual(OutputMode.rich, output.mode);\n   487→}\n   488→\n   489→test \"abbreviateStatus returns 4-char strings\" {\n   490→    const statuses = [_]Status{\n   491→        .open,\n   492→        .in_progress,\n   493→        .blocked,\n   494→        .deferred,\n   495→        .closed,\n   496→        .tombstone,\n   497→        .pinned,\n   498→        .{ .custom = \"test\" },\n   499→    };\n   500→    for (statuses) |status| {\n   501→        const abbrev = abbreviateStatus(status);\n   502→        try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 4), abbrev.len);\n   503→    }\n   504→}\n   505→\n   506→test \"priorityIndicator returns 3-char strings\" {\n   507→    var p: u3 = 0;\n   508→    while (p <= 4) : (p += 1) {\n   509→        const priority = Priority{ .value = p };\n   510→        const indicator = priorityIndicator(priority);\n   511→        try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 3), indicator.len);\n   512→    }\n   513→}\n   514→\n   515→test \"getStatusColor returns valid ANSI codes\" {\n   516→    const statuses = [_]Status{\n   517→        .open,\n   518→        .in_progress,\n   519→        .blocked,\n   520→        .deferred,\n   521→        .closed,\n   522→        .tombstone,\n   523→        .pinned,\n   524→        .{ .custom = \"test\" },\n   525→    };\n   526→    for (statuses) |status| {\n   527→        const color = getStatusColor(status);\n   528→        try std.testing.expect(color.len > 0);\n   529→        try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, color, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   530→    }\n   531→}\n   532→\n   533→test \"getPriorityColor returns valid ANSI codes\" {\n   534→    var p: u3 = 0;\n   535→    while (p <= 4) : (p += 1) {\n   536→        const priority = Priority{ .value = p };\n   537→        const color = getPriorityColor(priority);\n   538→        try std.testing.expect(color.len > 0);\n   539→        try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, color, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   540→    }\n   541→}\n   542→\n   543→test \"Color constants are valid ANSI escape sequences\" {\n   544→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.reset, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   545→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.bold, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   546→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.red, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   547→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.green, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   548→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.yellow, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   549→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.blue, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   550→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.gray, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   551→}\n   552→\n   553→test \"Output printIssueListQuiet writes IDs only\" {\n   554→    // Test the quiet formatting logic directly\n   555→    const issue1 = Issue.init(\"bd-abc123\", \"Test issue 1\", 1706540000);\n   556→    const issue2 = Issue.init(\"bd-def456\", \"Test issue 2\", 1706540000);\n   557→    const issues = [_]Issue{ issue1, issue2 };\n   558→\n   559→    // In quiet mode, printIssueListQuiet outputs \"{id}\\n\" for each issue\n   560→    // Verify the expected output format\n   561→    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"bd-abc123\", issue1.id);\n   562→    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"bd-def456\", issue2.id);\n   563→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 2), issues.len);\n   564→}\n   565→\n   566→test \"Output printIssueListPlain writes formatted lines\" {\n   567→    // Test the plain formatting logic via abbreviateStatus and Issue fields\n   568→    const issue = Issue.init(\"bd-abc123\", \"Test issue\", 1706540000);\n   569→\n   570→    // Verify issue fields are correct\n   571→    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"bd-abc123\", issue.id);\n   572→    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"Test issue\", issue.title);\n   573→    try std.testing.expectEqual(Status.open, issue.status);\n   574→\n   575→    // Verify status abbreviation\n   576→    const status_abbrev = abbreviateStatus(issue.status);\n   577→    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"OPEN\", status_abbrev);\n   578→}\n   579→\n   580→test \"Output printIssueListRich includes ANSI codes\" {\n   581→    // Test that rich mode formatting uses ANSI codes\n   582→    const issue = Issue.init(\"bd-abc123\", \"Test issue\", 1706540000);\n   583→\n   584→    // Verify issue fields\n   585→    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"bd-abc123\", issue.id);\n   586→\n   587→    // Verify rich mode uses color codes\n   588→    const status_color = getStatusColor(issue.status);\n   589→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, status_color, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   590→\n   591→    const priority_color = getPriorityColor(issue.priority);\n   592→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, priority_color, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   593→\n   594→    // Verify Color.bold is used\n   595→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, Color.bold, \"\\x1b[\"));\n   596→}\n   597→\n   598→test \"Output printIssueListJson produces valid JSON array\" {\n   599→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   600→\n   601→    // Test JSON serialization directly\n   602→    const issue1 = Issue.init(\"bd-abc123\", \"Test issue 1\", 1706540000);\n   603→    const issue2 = Issue.init(\"bd-def456\", \"Test issue 2\", 1706540000);\n   604→    const issues = [_]Issue{ issue1, issue2 };\n   605→\n   606→    // Serialize to JSON\n   607→    const json_bytes = try std.json.Stringify.valueAlloc(allocator, issues, .{});\n   608→    defer allocator.free(json_bytes);\n   609→\n   610→    // Verify it starts with [ and contains expected data\n   611→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.startsWith(u8, json_bytes, \"[\"));\n   612→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.indexOf(u8, json_bytes, \"bd-abc123\") != null);\n   613→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.indexOf(u8, json_bytes, \"bd-def456\") != null);\n   614→\n   615→    // Verify it can be parsed back\n   616→    const parsed = try std.json.parseFromSlice([]const Issue, allocator, json_bytes, .{});\n   617→    defer parsed.deinit();\n   618→    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 2), parsed.value.len);\n   619→}\n   620→\n   621→test \"Output.err formats error messages correctly\" {\n   622→    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n   623→\n   624→    // Test the error message formatting\n   625→    const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(allocator, \"error: \" ++ \"something went wrong: {s}\", .{\"test error\"});\n   626→    defer allocator.free(msg);\n   627→\n   628→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.indexOf(u8, msg, \"error:\") != null);\n   629→    try std.testing.expect(std.mem.indexOf(u8, msg, \"test error\") != null);\n Implement run() function with signature:\npub fn run(\n    command_args: CommandArgs,        // Parsed args specific to this command\n    global: args.GlobalOptions,       // Global flags\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n) !void\n```\n\n**Key Patterns in Command Implementation:**\n\n1. **Load workspace** using `CommandContext.init()` - returns null if not initialized\n2. **Validate inputs** - check required fields, valid enum values\n3. **Load store** - `CommandContext` provides pre-loaded `IssueStore`\n4. **Perform operation** - use store methods (insert, update, list, etc.)\n5. **Output results** - use `Output` formatter based on `global.isStructuredOutput()`\n6. **Auto-save** - call `ctx.saveIfAutoFlush()` if changes were made\n\n**Error handling**: Commands return specific error types and may return early with `.exit(1)` in dispatcher\n\n### 3. IssueStore Interface\n\n**Location:** `/home/hotschmoe/beads_zig/src/storage/store.zig`\n\nIn-memory store with persistence to JSONL:\n\n**Key Methods:**\n\n```zig\n// Initialization\npub fn init(allocator, jsonl_path) IssueStore\npub fn deinit()\npub fn loadFromFile() !void\npub fn saveToFile() !void\n\n// CRUD Operations\npub fn insert(issue: Issue) !void\npub fn get(id: []const u8) !?Issue              // Returns clone\npub fn getRef(id: []const u8) ?*Issue          // Returns reference (no clone)\npub fn update(id, updates: IssueUpdate, now: i64) !void\npub fn delete(id, now: i64) !void              // Soft delete (sets tombstone)\npub fn exists(id: []const u8) !bool\n\n// Querying\npub const ListFilters = struct {\n    status: ?Status = null,\n    priority: ?Priority = null,\n    issue_type: ?IssueType = null,\n    assignee: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    label: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    include_tombstones: bool = false,\n    limit: ?u32 = null,\n    offset: ?u32 = null,\n    order_by: OrderBy = .created_at,\n    order_desc: bool = true,\n};\npub fn list(filters: ListFilters) ![]Issue\n\n// Aggregation\npub fn count(group_by: ?GroupBy) ![]CountResult\n\n// Relations\npub fn getLabels(issue_id: []const u8) ![][]const u8\npub fn addLabel(issue_id, label) !void\npub fn removeLabel(issue_id, label) !void\npub fn getComments(issue_id: []const u8) ![]Comment\npub fn addComment(issue_id, comment: Comment) !void\npub fn getDependencies(issue_id) ![]Dependency\n\n// Dirty tracking (for sync/export)\npub fn markDirty(id) !void\npub fn clearDirty(id) !void\npub fn getDirtyIds() ![][]const u8\npub fn isDirty() bool\n```\n\n**Important Notes:**\n- `update()` takes an `IssueUpdate` struct with optional fields (only set fields are updated)\n- `list()` returns cloned issues; caller must free with `deinit()` on each\n- Filtering with `include_tombstones: false` by default (soft deletes are hidden)\n- Dirty tracking marks issues modified since last save\n\n### 4. Output Formatting\n\n**Location:** `/home/hotschmoe/beads_zig/src/output/mod.zig`\n\nUnified output interface:\n\n```zig\npub const OutputOptions = struct {\n    json: bool = false,\n    toon: bool = false,\n    quiet: bool = false,\n    no_color: bool = false,\n};\n\npub const Output = struct {\n    // Initialize with options\n    pub fn init(allocator, opts: OutputOptions) Output\n    \n    // Issue display\n    pub fn printIssue(issue: Issue) !void\n    pub fn printIssueList(issues: []const Issue) !void\n    \n    // Generic messages\n    pub fn println(comptime fmt, args) !void\n    pub fn print(comptime fmt, args) !void\n    pub fn success(comptime fmt, args) !void\n    pub fn err(comptime fmt, args) !void\n    pub fn warn(comptime fmt, args) !void\n    pub fn info(comptime fmt, args) !void\n    \n    // JSON output\n    pub fn printJson(value: anytype) !void\n};\n```\n\n**Output Modes:**\n- **plain**: No colors, basic formatting\n- **rich**: ANSI colors for TTY (auto-detected)\n- **json**: JSON output (triggered by `--json` or `--toon` flags)\n- **quiet**: Minimal output (IDs only)\n\n**TOON Mode**: When `--toon` flag is set, JSON is converted to token-optimized format via `toon_zig` library\n\n### 5.   }\n   343→\n   344→    /// Parse all arguments into a ParseResult.\n   345→    pub fn parse(self: *Self) ParseError!ParseResult {\n   346→        var global = GlobalOptions{};\n   347→\n   348→        // Parse global flags first\n   349→        while (self.hasNext()) {\n   350→            const arg = self.peek().?;\n   351→            if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, arg, \"-\")) {\n   352→                if (self.parseGlobalFlag(&global)) |consumed| {\n   353→                    if (!consumed) break;\n   354→                } else |_| {\n   355→                    break;\n   356→                }\n   357→            } else {\n   358→                break;\n   359→            }\n   360→        }\n   361→\n   362→        // Parse subcommand\n   363→        const cmd_str = self.next() orelse {\n   364→            return .{\n   365→                .global = global,\n   366→                .command = .{ .help = .{ .topic = null } },\n   367→            };\n   368→        };\n   369→\n   370→        const command = try self.parseCommand(cmd_str);\n   371→\n   372→        return .{\n   373→            .global = global,\n   374→            .command = command,\n   375→        };\n   376→    }\n   377→\n   378→    fn parseGlobalFlag(self: *Self, global: *GlobalOptions) ParseError!bool {\n   379→        const arg = self.next().?;\n   380→\n   381→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--json\")) {\n   382→            global.json = true;\n   383→            return true;\n   384→        }\n   385→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--toon\")) {\n   386→            global.toon = true;\n   387→            return true;\n   388→        }\n   389→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"-q\") or std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--quiet\")) {\n   390→            global.quiet = true;\n   391→            return true;\n   392→        }\n   393→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"-v\") or std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--verbose\")) {\n   394→            global.verbose +|= 1;\n   395→            return true;\n   396→        }\n   397→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"-vv\")) {\n   398→            global.verbose +|= 2;\n   399→            return true;\n   400→        }\n   401→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--no-color\")) {\n   402→            global.no_color = true;\n   403→            return true;\n   404→        }\n   405→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--no-auto-flush\")) {\n   406→            global.no_auto_flush = true;\n   407→            return true;\n   408→        }\n   409→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--no-auto-import\")) {\n   410→            global.no_auto_import = true;\n   411→            return true;\n   412→        }\n   413→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--data\") or std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--db\")) {\n   414→            global.data_path = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n   415→            return true;\n   416→        }\n   417→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--actor\")) {\n   418→            global.actor = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n   423→            global.lock_timeout = std.fmt.parseInt(u32, val, 10) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n   424→            return true;\n   425→        }\n   426→\n   427→        // Put back if not recognized\n   428→        self.index -= 1;\n   429→        return error.UnknownFlag;\n   430→    }\n   431→\n   432→    fn parseCommand(self: *Self, cmd: []const u8) ParseError!Command {\n   433→        // Workspace\n   434→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"init\")) {\n   435→            return .{ .init = try self.parseInitArgs() };\n   436→        }\n   437→       return self.index < self.args.len;\n   894→    }\n   895→\n   896→    fn peek(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n   897→        if (self.index >= self.args.len) return null;\n   898→        return self.args[self.index];\n   899→    }\n   900→\n   901→    fn next(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n   902→        if (self.index >= self.args.len) return null;\n   903→        const arg = self.args[self.index];\n   904→        self.index += 1;\n   905→        return arg;\n   906→    }\n   907→\n   908→    /// Skip a peeked argument (used after checking with peek() and wanting to consume it).\n   909→    fn skip(self: *Self) void {\n   910→        if (self.index < self.args.len) {\n   911→            self.index += 1;\n   912→        }\n   913→    }\n   914→\n   915→    /// Check if current arg matches a flag, and if so consume it and return true.\n   916→    fn consumeFlag(self: *Self, short: ?[]const u8, long: []const u8) bool {\n   917→        const arg = self.peek() orelse return false;\n   918→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, long) or (short != null and std.mem.eql(u8, arg, short.?))) {\n   919→            self.skip();\n   920→            return true;\n   921→        }\n   922→        return false;\n   923→    }\n   924→\n   925→    /// Parse a u32 value after consuming a flag. Returns null if missing, error if invalid.\n   926→    fn consumeU32(self: *Self) ParseError!?u32 {\n   927→        const val = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n   928→        return std.fmt.parseInt(u32, val, 10) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n   929→    }\n   930→\n   931→    /// Parse an optional --limit/-n flag, returning the value if present.\n   932→    fn parseLimitFlag(self: *Self) ParseError!?u32 {\n   933→        if (self.consumeFlag(\"-n\", \"--limit\")) {\n   934→            return try self.consumeU32();\n   935→        }\n   936→        return null;\n   937→    }\n   938→\n   939→    /// Returns the next arg if it's a positional (doesn't start with \"-\"), otherwise null.\n   940→    fn peekPositional(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n   941→        const arg = self.peek() orelse return null;\n   942→        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, arg, \"-\")) return null;\n   943→        return arg;\n   944→    }\n   945→};\n   946→\n   947→// Tests\n Supports global flags, subcommands, and subcommand-specific arguments.\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\n\n/// Global CLI options that apply to all commands.\npub const GlobalOptions = struct {\n    json: bool = false,\n    toon: bool = false,\n    quiet: bool = false,\n    verbose: u8 = 0,\n    no_color: bool = false,\n    data_path: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    actor: ?[]const u8 = null,\n (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"bash\")) return .bash;\n        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"zsh\")) return .zsh;\n        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"fish\")) return .fish;\n        if command,\n        };\n    }\n\n    fn parseGlobalFlag(self: *Self, global: *GlobalOptions) ParseError!bool {\n        const arg = self.next().?;\n\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--json\")) {\n            global.json = true;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--toon\")) {\n            global.toon = true;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"-q\") or std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--quiet\")) {\n            global.quiet = true;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"-v\") or std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--verbose\")) {\n            global.verbose +|= 1;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"-vv\")) {\n            global.verbose +|= 2;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--no-color\")) {\n            global.no_color = true;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"blocked\")) {\n            return .{ .blocked = try self.parseBlockedArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"search\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"completions\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"completion\")) {\n            return .{ .completions = try self.parseCompletionsArgs() };\n        }\n\n        // Help\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"help\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"--help\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"-h\")) {\n            return .{ .help = try self.parseHelpArgs() };\n        }\n\n        return error.UnknownCommand;\n    }\n\n    fn parseInitArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!InitArgs {\n        var result = InitArgs{};\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-p\", \"--prefix\")) {\n                result.prefix = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                result.prefix = self.next().?;\n            } else break;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseCreateArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!CreateArgs {\n        var result = CreateArgs{ .title = undefined };\n        var title_set = false;\n        var labels: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n        var deps: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-d\", \"--description\")) {\n                result.description = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-t\", \"--type\")) {\n                result.issue_type = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-p\", \"--priority\")) {\n                result.priority = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-a\", \"--assignee\")) {\n                result.assignee = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-l\", \"--label\")) {\n                labels.append(self.allocator, self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"--depends-on\", \"--dep\")) {\n                deps.append(self.allocator, self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(null, \"--due\")) {\n                result.due = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-e\", \"--estimate\")) {\n                const val = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n                result.estimate = std.fmt.parseInt(i32, val, 10) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n            } else if (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                if (!title_set) {\n                    result.title = self.next().?;\n                    title_set = true;\n                } else break;\n            } else break;\n        }\n\n        if (!title_set) return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n\n        if (labels.items.len > 0) {\n            result.labels = labels.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n        }\n        if (deps.items.len > 0) {\n            result.deps = deps.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n        }\n\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseQuickArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!QuickArgs {\n        var result = QuickArgs{ .title = undefined };\n        var title_set = false;\n\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-p\", \"--priority\")) {\n                result.priority = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                if (!title_set) {\n                    result.title = self.next().?;\n                    title_set = true;\n                } else break;\n            } else break;\n        }\n\n        if (!title_set) return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseShowArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!ShowArgs {\n        const id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        return .{ .id = id };\n    }\n\n    fn parseUpdateArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!UpdateArgs {\n        var result = UpdateArgs{ .id = undefined };\n        var id_set = false;\n\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(null, \"--title\")) {\n                result.title = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-d\", \"--description\")) {\n                result.description = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-t\", \"--type\")) {\n                result.issue_type = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-p\", \"--priority\")) {\n                result.priority = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-a\", \"--assignee\")) {\n                result.assignee = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-s\", \"--status\")) {\n                result.status = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                if (!id_set) {\n                    result.id = self.next().?;\n                    id_set = true;\n                } else break;\n            } else break;\n        }\n\n        if (!id_set) return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseCloseArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!CloseArgs {\n        var result = CloseArgs{ .id = undefined };\n        var id_set = false;\n\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-r\", \"--reason\")) {\n                result.reason = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                if error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseReopenArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!ReopenArgs {\n        const id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        return .{ .id = id };\n    }\n\n    fn parseListArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!ListArgs {\n        var result = ListArgs{};\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-s\", \"--status\")) {\n                result.status = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-p\", \"--priority\")) {\n                result.priority = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-t\", \"--type\")) {\n                result.issue_type = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-a\", \"--assignee\")) {\n                result.assignee = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-l\", \"--label\")) {\n                result.label = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (try self.parseLimitFlag()) |limit| {\n                result.limit = limit;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-A\", \"--all\")) {\n                result.all = true;\n            } else break;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseReadyArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!ReadyArgs {\n        var result = ReadyArgs{};\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (try self.parseLimitFlag()) |limit| {\n                result.limit = limit;\n            } else break;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseBlockedArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!BlockedArgs {\n        var result = BlockedArgs{};\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (try self.parseLimitFlag()) |limit| {\n                result.limit = limit;\n            } else break;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseSearchArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!SearchArgs {\n        var result = SearchArgs{ .query = undefined };\n        var query_set = false;\n\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (try self.parseLimitFlag()) |limit| {\n                result.limit = limit;\n            } else if (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                if (!query_set) {\n                    result.query = self.next().?;\n                    query_set = true;\n                } else break;\n            } else break;\n        }\n\n        if (!query_set) return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseStaleArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!StaleArgs {\n        var result = StaleArgs{};\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-d\", \"--days\")) {\n                result.days = try self.consumeU32() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (try self.parseLimitFlag()) |limit| {\n                result.limit = limit;\n            } else break;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseCountArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!CountArgs {\n        var result = CountArgs{};\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-g\", \"--group-by\")) {\n                result.group_by = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else break;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseDepArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!DepArgs {\n        const subcmd = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"add\")) {\n            const child = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n            const parent = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n            var dep_type: []const u8 = \"blocks\";\n            while (self.hasNext()) {\n                if (self.consumeFlag(\"-t\", \"--type\")) {\n                    dep_type = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n                } else break;\n            }\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .add = .{ .child = child, .parent = parent, .dep_type = dep_type } } };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"remove\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"rm\")) {\n            const child = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n            const parent = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .remove = .{ .child = child, .parent = parent } } };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"list\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"ls\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .list = .{ .id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument } } };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"tree\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .tree = .{ .id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument } } };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"cycles\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .cycles = {} } };\n        }\n        return error.UnknownSubcommand;\n    }\n\n    fn parseLabelArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!LabelArgs {\n        const subcmd = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"add\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"remove\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"rm\")) {\n            const is_add = std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"add\");\n            const id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n            var labels: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n\n            while (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                labels.append(self.allocator, self.next().?) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n            }\n\n            if (labels.items.len == 0) return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n\n            const label_slice = labels.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n            if (is_add) {\n                return .{ .subcommand = .{ .add = .{ .id = id, .labels = label_slice } } };\n            } else {\n                return .{ .subcommand = .{ .remove = .{ .id = id, .labels = label_slice } } };\n            }\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"list\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"ls\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .list = .{ .id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument } } };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"list-all\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"all\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .list_all = {} } };\n        }\n        return error.UnknownSubcommand;\n    }\n\n    fn parseCommentsArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!CommentsArgs {\n        const subcmd = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"add\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .add = .{\n                .id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument,\n                .text = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument,\n            } } };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"list\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"ls\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .list = .{  const id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        return .{ .id = id };\n    }\n\n    fn parseAuditArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!AuditArgs {\n        var result = result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseSyncArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!SyncArgs {\n        var result = SyncArgs{};\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"--export\", \"--flush-only\")) {\n                result.flush_only = true;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"--import\", \"--import-only\")) {\n                result.import_only = true;\n            } else break;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseCompletionsArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!CompletionsArgs {\n        const shell_str = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        const shell = Shell.fromString(shell_str) orelse return error.InvalidShell;\n        return .{ .shell = shell };\n    }\n\n    fn parseHelpArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!HelpArgs {\n        return .{ .topic = self.next() };\n    }\n\n    fn parseConfigArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!ConfigArgs {\n        const subcmd = self.next() orelse return .{ .subcommand = .{ .list = {} } };\n\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"get\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .get = .{ .key = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument } } };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"set\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .set = .{\n                .key = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument,\n                .value = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument,\n            } } };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"list\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"ls\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .list = {} } };\n        }\n        return error.UnknownSubcommand;\n    }\n\n    fn hasNext(self: *Self) bool {\n        return self.index < self.args.len;\n    }\n\n    fn peek(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n        if (self.index >= self.args.len) return null;\n        return self.args[self.index];\n    }\n\n    fn next(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n        if (self.index >= self.args.len) return null;\n        const arg = self.args[self.index];\n        self.index += 1;\n        return arg;\n    }\n\n    /// Skip a peeked argument (used after checking with peek() and wanting to consume it).\n    fn skip(self: *Self) void {\n        if (self.index < self.args.len) {\n            self.index += 1;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Check if current arg matches a flag, and if so consume it and return true.\n    fn consumeFlag(self: *Self, short: ?[]const u8, long: []const u8) bool {\n        const arg = self.peek() orelse return false;\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, long) or (short != null and std.mem.eql(u8, arg, short.?))) {\n            self.skip();\n            return true;\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /// Parse a u32 value after consuming a flag. Returns null if missing, error if invalid.\n    fn consumeU32(self: *Self) ParseError!?u32 {\n        const val = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n        return std.fmt.parseInt(u32, val, 10) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n    }\n\n    /// Parse an optional --limit/-n flag, returning the value if present.\n    fn parseLimitFlag(self: *Self) ParseError!?u32 {\n        if (self.consumeFlag(\"-n\", \"--limit\")) {\n            return try self.consumeU32();\n        }\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    /// Returns the next arg if it's a positional (doesn't start with \"-\"), otherwise null.\n    fn peekPositional(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n        const arg = self.peek() orelse return null;\n        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, arg, \"-\")) return null;\n        return arg;\n    }\n};\n\n// Tests\n\ntest \"parse no arguments shows help\" {\n    const args = [_][]const u8{};\n    var parser = ArgParser.init(std.testing.allocator, &args);\n    const result = try parser.parse();\n\n    try std.testing.expect(result.command == .help);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(?[]const u8, null), result.command.help.topic);\n}\n\ntest Provides workspace loading, error handling, and shared result types\n//! to reduce duplication across command implementations.\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst storage = @import(\"../storage/mod.zig\");\nconst output_mod = @import(\"../output/mod.zig\");\nconst args = @import(\"args.zig\");\n\npub const Output = output_mod.Output;\npub const OutputOptions = output_mod.OutputOptions;\npub const IssueStore = storage.IssueStore;\npub const DependencyGraph = storage.DependencyGraph;\n\n/// Common errors shared across CLI commands.\npub const CommandError = error{\n    WorkspaceNotInitialized,\n    StorageError,\n    OutOfMemory,\n};\n\n/// Context for executing a CLI command with an initialized workspace.\npub const CommandContext = struct {\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    output: Output,\n    store: IssueStore,\n    issues_path: []const u8,\n    global: args.GlobalOptions,\n\n    /// Initialize a command context by loading the workspace.\n    /// Returns null and outputs an error if workspace is not initialized.\n    pub fn init(\n        allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n        global: args.GlobalOptions,\n    ) CommandError!?CommandContext {\n        var output = Output.init(allocator, .{\n            .json = global.json,\n            .toon = global.toon,\n            .quiet = global.quiet,\n            .no_color = global.no_color,\n        });\n\n        const beads_dir = global.data_path orelse \".beads\";\n        const issues_path = std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ beads_dir, \"issues.jsonl\" }) catch {\n            return CommandError.OutOfMemory;\n        };\n\n        std.fs.cwd().access(issues_path, .{}) catch |err| {\n            if (err == error.FileNotFound) {\n                outputErrorGeneric(&output, global.isStructuredOutput(), \"workspace not initialized. \"cannot access workspace\") catch {};\n            allocator.free(issues_path);\n            return CommandError.StorageError;\n        };\n\n        var store = IssueStore.init(allocator, issues_path);\n\n        store.loadFromFile() catch |err| {\n            if (err != error.FileNotFound) {\n                outputErrorGeneric(&output, global.isStructuredOutput(), \"failed to load issues\") catch {};\n                store.deinit();\n                allocator.free(issues_path);\n                return CommandError.StorageError;\n            }\n        };\n\n        return  stdout: std.fs.File,\n    70→    stderr: std.fs.File,\n    71→    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    72→\n    73→    const Self = @This();\n    74→\n    75→    /// Initialize output formatter based on global options and TTY detection.\n    76→    pub fn init(allocator: std.mem.Allocator, opts: OutputOptions) Self {\n    77→        const stdout = std.fs.File.stdout();\n    78→        const stderr = std.fs.File.stderr();\n    79→\n    80→        var mode: OutputMode = .plain;\n    81→        if (opts.json or opts.toon) {\n    82→            mode = .json;\n    83→        } else if (opts.quiet) {\n    84→            mode = .quiet;\n    85→        } else if (!opts.no_color and !checkNoColorEnv() and stdout.isTty()) {\n    86→            mode = .rich;\n    87→        }\n    88→\n    89→        return .{\n    90→            .mode = mode,\n    91→            .toon = opts.toon,\n    92→            .stdout = stdout,\n    93→            .stderr = stderr,\n    94→            .allocator = 147→\n   148→    /// Print a formatted message to stdout.\n   149→    pub fn print(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n   150→        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n   151→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt, args);\n   152→        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n   153→        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n   154→    }\n   155→\n   156→    /// Print a formatted message to stdout with newline.\n   157→    pub fn println(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n   158→        if (self.mode == .quiet) self.allocator.free(msg);\n   180→        try self.stderr.writeAll(msg);\n   181→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stderr.writeAll(Color.reset);\n   182→        try anytype) !void {\n   187→        if (self.mode == .quiet) return;\n   188→        if (self.mode == .rich) try self.stderr.writeAll(Color.yellow);\n   189→        const msg = try 200→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt, args);\n   201→        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n   202→        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n   203→        if (self.mode /// If toon mode is enabled, converts JSON to TOON format for reduced token usage.\n   214→    pub fn printJson(self: *Self, value: anytype) !void {\n   215→        const json_bytes = try @import(\"toon_zig\");\n   220→            const toon_bytes = toon.jsonToToon(self.allocator, json_bytes) catch |convert_err| {\n   221→                try self.stderr.writeAll(\"error: failed to convert to TOON format\\n\");\n   222→                return convert_err;\n   223→            };\n   224→            defer self.allocator.free(toon_bytes);\n   225→            try self.stdout.writeAll(toon_bytes);\n   226→        } else {\n   227→            try self.stdout.writeAll(json_bytes);\n   228→        }\n   229→        try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   230→    }\n   231→\n   232→    // ========================================================================\n   233→    // JSON Mode Helpers\n   234→    // ========================================================================\n   235→\n   236→    fn printIssueJson(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n   237→        try self.printJson(issue);\n   238→    }\n   239→\n   240→    fn printIssueListJson(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n   241→        try self.printJson(issues);\n   242→    }\n   243→\n   244→    // ========================================================================\n   245→    // Plain Mode Helpers\n   246→    // ========================================================================\n   247→\n   248→    fn printIssuePlain(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n   249→        try self.writeFormatted(\"ID: {s}\\n\", .{issue.id});\n   250→        try self.writeFormatted(\"Title: {s}\\n\", .{issue.title});\n   251→        try self.writeFormatted(\"Status: {s}\\n\", .{issue.status.toString()});\n   252→        try self.writeFormatted(\"Priority: {s}\\n\", .{issue.priority.toString()});\n   253→        try self.writeFormatted(\"Type: {s}\\n\", .{issue.issue_type.toString()});\n   254→\n   255→        if (issue.description) |desc| {\n   256→            try self.writeFormatted(\"Description: {s}\\n\", .{desc});\n   257→        }\n   258→        if (issue.assignee) |assignee| {\n   259→            try self.writeFormatted(\"Assignee: {s}\\n\", .{assignee});\n   260→        }\n   261→        if (issue.labels.len > 0) {\n   262→            try self.stdout.writeAll(\"Labels: \");\n   263→            for (issue.labels, 0..) |label, i| {\n   264→                if (i > 0) try self.stdout.writeAll(\", \");\n   265→                try self.stdout.writeAll(label);\n   266→            }\n   267→            try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   268→        }\n   269→        if (issue.due_at.value) |due| {\n   270→            try self.writeFormatted(\"Due: {d}\\n\", .{due});\n   271→        }\n   272→\n   273→        try self.writeFormatted(\"Created: {d}\\n\", .{issue.created_at.value});\n   274→        try self.writeFormatted(\"Updated: {d}\\n\", .{issue.updated_at.value});\n   275→    }\n   276→\n   277→    fn printIssueListPlain(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n   278→        for (issues) |issue| {\n   279→            const status_abbrev = abbreviateStatus(issue.status);\n   280→            try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}  [{s}] {s}\\n\", .{\n   281→                issue.id,\n   282→                status_abbrev,\n   283→                issue.title,\n   284→            });\n   285→        }\n   286→    }\n   287→\n   288→    // ========================================================================\n   289→    // Rich Mode Helpers (ANSI colors)\n   290→    // ========================================================================\n   291→\n   292→    fn printIssueRich(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n   293→        // Bold ID\n   294→        try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ Color.bold, issue.id, Color.reset });\n   295→\n   296→        // Title\n   297→        try self.writeFormatted(\"  {s}\\n\", .{issue.title});\n   298→\n   299→        // Status with color\n   300→        const status_color = getStatusColor(issue.status);\n   301→        try self.writeFormatted(\"  Status: {s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ status_color, issue.status.toString(), Color.reset });\n   302→\n   303→        // Priority with color\n   304→        const priority_color = getPriorityColor(issue.priority);\n   305→        try self.writeFormatted(\"  Priority: {s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ priority_color, issue.priority.toString(), Color.reset });\n   306→\n   307→        // Type\n   308→        try self.writeFormatted(\"  Type: {s}\\n\", .{issue.issue_type.toString()});\n   309→\n   310→        // Optional fields\n   311→        if (issue.description) |desc| {\n   312→            try self.writeFormatted(\"  Description: {s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ Color.dim, desc, Color.reset });\n   313→        }\n   314→        if (issue.assignee) |assignee| {\n   315→            try self.writeFormatted(\"  Assignee: {s}{s}{s}\\n\", .{ Color.cyan, assignee, Color.reset });\n   316→        }\n   317→        if (issue.labels.len > 0) {\n   318→            try self.stdout.writeAll(\"  Labels: \");\n   319→            for (issue.labels, 0..) |label, i| {\n   320→                if (i > 0) try self.stdout.writeAll(\", \");\n   321→                try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}{s}{s}\", .{ Color.magenta, label, Color.reset });\n   322→            }\n   323→            try self.stdout.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   324→        }\n   325→    }\n   326→\n   327→    fn printIssueListRich(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n   328→        for (issues) |issue| {\n   329→            const status_color = getStatusColor(issue.status);\n   330→            const priority_color = getPriorityColor(issue.priority);\n   331→            const status_abbrev = abbreviateStatus(issue.status);\n   332→\n   333→            try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}{s}{s}  {s}[{s}]{s}  {s}{s}{s}  {s}\\n\", .{\n   334→                Color.bold,\n   335→                issue.id,\n   336→                Color.reset,\n   337→                status_color,\n   338→                status_abbrev,\n   339→                Color.reset,\n   340→                priority_color,\n   341→                priorityIndicator(issue.priority),\n   342→                Color.reset,\n   343→                issue.title,\n   344→            });\n   345→        }\n   346→    }\n   347→\n   348→    // ========================================================================\n   349→    // Quiet Mode Helpers\n   350→    // ========================================================================\n   351→\n   352→    fn printIssueQuiet(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n   353→        try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}\\n\", .{issue.id});\n   354→    }\n   355→\n   356→    fn printIssueListQuiet(self: *Self, issues: []const Issue) !void {\n   357→        for (issues) |issue| {\n   358→            try self.writeFormatted(\"{s}\\n\", .{issue.id});\n   359→        }\n   360→    }\n   361→\n   362→    // ========================================================================\n   363→    // Internal Helpers\n   364→    // ========================================================================\n   365→\n   366→    fn writeFormatted(self: *Self, comptime fmt: []const u8, args: anytype) !void {\n   367→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(self.allocator, fmt, args);\n   368→        defer self.allocator.free(msg);\n   369→        try self.stdout.writeAll(msg);\n   370→    }\n   371→};\n   372→\n   373→// ============================================================================\n   374→// Helper Functions\n   375→// ============================================================================\n   376→\n   377→/// Check if NO_COLOR environment variable is set (cross-platform).\n   378→fn checkNoColorEnv() bool {\n   379→    // Per NO_COLOR spec, only existence matters, not the value\n   380→    return std.process.hasEnvVarConstant(\"NO_COLOR\");\n   381→}\n   382→\n   383→/// Get ANSI color for a status.\n   384→fn getStatusColor(status: Status) []const u8 {\n   385→    return switch (status) {\n   386→        .open => Color.green,\n   387→        .in_progress => Color.yellow,\n   388→        .blocked => Color.red,\n   389→        .deferred => Color.gray,\n   390→        .closed => Color.gray,\n   391→        .tombstone => Color.dim,\n   392→        .pinned => Color.bright_cyan,\n   393→        .custom => Color.blue,\n   394→    };\n   395→}\n   396→\n   397→/// Get ANSI color for a priority.\n   398→fn getPriorityColor(priority: Priority) []const u8 {\n   399→    return switch (priority.value) {\n   400→        0 => Color.bright_red, // critical\n   401→        1 => Color.red, // high\n   402→        2 => Color.yellow, // medium\n   403→        3 => Color.green, // low\n   404→        4 => Color.gray, // backlog\n   405→        else => Color.reset,\n   406→    };\n   407→}\n   408→\n   409→/// Get short status abbreviation.\n   410→fn abbreviateStatus(status: Status) []const u8 {\n   411→    return switch (status) {\n   412→        .open => \"OPEN\",\n   413→        .in_progress => \"PROG\",\n   414→        .blocked => \"BLKD\",\n   415→        .deferred => \"DEFR\",\n   416→        .closed => \"DONE\",\n   417→        .tombstone => \"DEL \",\n   418→        .pinned => \"PIN \",\n   419→        .custom => \"CUST\",\n   420→    };\n   421→}\n   422→\n   423→/// Get priority indicator symbol.\n   424→fn priorityIndicator(priority: Priority) []const u8 {\n   425→    return switch (priority.value) {\n   426→        0 => \"!!!\",\n   427→        1 => \"!! \",\n   428→        2 => \"!  \",\n   429→        3 => \".  \",\n   430→        4 => \"   \",\n   431→        else => \"   \",\n   432→    };\n   433→}\n   434→\n   435→//
